	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js') != 'fbac7de1230e93ab2429e4ce11bb11fbcae4c468') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js') !== 'fbac7de1230e93ab2429e4ce11bb11fbcae4c468') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js') !== '426a225b70eaa442783e10e568cd26e5e0f07430') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js') !== 'fbac7de1230e93ab2429e4ce11bb11fbcae4c468') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'f900fc0d56cafea4c10d019a57de31b294046e12') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f900fc0d56cafea4c10d019a57de31b294046e12') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f8118025406c2204ee3bd826e6b0e02540acf772') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f900fc0d56cafea4c10d019a57de31b294046e12') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 658\n");
